    name: system-name, type: STRING
    name: hostname, type: STRING
    name: appname, type: STRING
    name: processid, type: UINT32
    name: threadid, type: UINT32
    name: filename, type: STRING
    name: linenumber, type: UINT32

2.1.1.1.1  list rw-ui:debug-details
  Leaves
    name: type, type: IDREF, description: Kind of debug data.
    name: details, type: STRING, description: Detailed debug information for the event, such as stack trace.
    This information is intended for detailed debugging and might
    not contain end-user relevant information.
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:debug-details
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:debug-details[rw-ui:type='generic-debug-detail']
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/template_params/debug-details/generic-debug-detail
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:debug-details
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:debug-details[rw-ui:type='generic-debug-detail']
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.GenericDebug.TemplateParams.DebugDetails
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_DebugDetails
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type

2.1.1.1.2  list rw-ui:additional-data
  Leaves
    name: attribute, type: STRING, description: The name of the attribute
    name: value, type: STRING, description: Additional data that could not be captured according to the
    schema.  This information may contain debugging details
    relevant to the end-user.
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:additional-data
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:additional-data[rw-ui:attribute='STRING']
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/template_params/additional-data/STRING
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:additional-data

2.1.1.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:generic-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-debug/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.GenericDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__GenericDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.4.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:generic-warning/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:generic-warning/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:generic-warning/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-warning/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-warning/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.GenericWarning.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__GenericWarning__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.7.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:generic-alert/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:generic-alert/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:generic-alert/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-alert/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:generic-alert/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.GenericAlert.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_GenericAlert_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__GenericAlert__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_GenericAlert_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_GenericAlert_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_GenericAlert_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.10.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:project-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:project-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:project-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:project-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:project-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.ProjectInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_ProjectInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__ProjectInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_ProjectInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_ProjectInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_ProjectInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.13.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:project-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:project-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:project-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:project-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:project-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.ProjectError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_ProjectError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__ProjectError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_ProjectError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_ProjectError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_ProjectError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.16.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:project-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:project-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:project-emergency/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:project-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:project-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.ProjectEmergency.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_ProjectEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__ProjectEmergency__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_ProjectEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_ProjectEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsd-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsd-info/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.NsdInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_NsdInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__NsdInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.19.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-notice/template_params/call-identifier

2.1.21.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.NsdError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_NsdError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__NsdError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_NsdError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_NsdError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.24.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:nsd-emergency/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.NsdEmergency.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_NsdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__NsdEmergency__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_NsdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_NsdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_NsdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.27.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfd-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfd-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.VnfdNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_VnfdNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__VnfdNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfd-error/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.VnfdError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_VnfdError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__VnfdError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.30.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier

2.1.32.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:vnfd-emergency/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfd-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.VnfdEmergency.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_VnfdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__VnfdEmergency__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_VnfdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_VnfdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_VnfdEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.35.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.NsrNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_NsrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__NsrNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_NsrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_NsrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_NsrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.38.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-critical/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.NsrCritical.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_NsrCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__NsrCritical__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:nsr-emergency/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsr-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:nsr-emergency/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.NsrEmergency.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_NsrEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__NsrEmergency__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.43.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:vnfr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:vnfr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:vnfr-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfr-notice/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.VnfrNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_VnfrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__VnfrNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_VnfrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_VnfrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_VnfrNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.46.1.3  container rw-ui:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rw-ui:vnfr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rw-ui:vnfr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-ui:vnfr-critical/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rw-ui:vnfr-critical/rw-ui:template_params/rw-ui:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_ui.YangNotif.RwUi.VnfrCritical.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwUiYang.YangNotif_RwUi_VnfrCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwUi__YangNotif__RwUi__VnfrCritical__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwUi_RwUi_notif_VnfrCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwUi_notif_VnfrCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwUi_RwUi_notif_VnfrCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
